#!/bin/bash

# Check if running as root
if [ "$EUID" -ne 0 ]; then
  echo "Please run as root"
  exit 1
fi

# Install certbot if not already installed
if ! command -v certbot &> /dev/null; then
    echo "Installing certbot..."
    apt-get update
    apt-get install -y certbot
fi

# Prompt for the IP address
read -p "Enter the IP address: " ip_address

# Validate IP address format
if ! [[ $ip_address =~ ^[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+\.[0-9]+$ ]]; then
    echo "Invalid IP address format"
    exit 1
fi

# Run certbot to obtain the certificate
certbot certonly --standalone -d $ip_address --agree-tos --email admin@example.com

# Check if certificate was obtained successfully
if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
    echo "SSL certificate obtained successfully for $ip_address"
    echo "Certificate location: /etc/letsencrypt/live/$ip_address/"
else
    echo "Failed to obtain SSL certificate"
fi
